Wishing you all a very happy new year.

The Indian Web3 ecosystem is growing exponentially, and we feel it is the right time to explore and start your entrepreneurial journey and hence Kludge is collaborating with woodstock for a masterclass on blockchain technology on *20th january, 2023 at 6pm IST*. 

Woodstock is launching Woodstock Labs, an incubation arm which will help new ideas grow and mentor.

Woodstock Labs is a new incubation program to support high-potential founders with the best resources to help them jump-start their ideas. We aim to bring together the finest resources from our network and help establish market-ready Web 3.0 startups by leveraging our global network of mentors with experience in building pillars of the core blockchain development suite and a diverse array of industry partners.

Woodstock would like to conduct a *Masterclass on Blockchain 101 - Understanding the Basics of Web3 Stack* and interact with students interested in going deeper into the Web3 world. The session will be hosted by Abhinav Pathak, Research Partner and Divesh Agarwal, Communications and Partnership Lead at Woodstock.
